    SELECT [e0].[ParticipantId], [e0].[EventId], [e0].[RegisteredAt], [e0].[UserId], [u].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[DepartmentId], [u].[DisabilityStatus], [u].[Email], [u].[Gender], [u].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [u].[Name], [u].[Nationality], [u].[Password], [u].[PasswordResetToken], [u].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[Role], [u].[SchoolNumber], [u].[Surname], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[TwoFactorSecret]

ORDER BY [e].[EventId], [c].[ClubId], [s].[ParticipantId]

SELECT [e].[EventId], [e].[Category], [e].[ClubId], [e].[CreatedAt], [e].[Description], [e].[EndDate], [e].[Image], [e].[ImageUrl], [e].[MaxParticipants], [e].[Name], [e].[ParticipantCount], [e].[StartDate], [e].[Status], [e].[UpdatedAt], [c].[ClubId], [c].[AdvisorId], [c].[CategoryId], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[Description], [c].[Document], [c].[EventCount], [c].[Image], [c].[MemberCount], [c].[Name], [c].[Status], [s].[ParticipantId], [s].[EventId], [s].[RegisteredAt], [s].[UserId], [s].[UserId0], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[DepartmentId], [s].[DisabilityStatus], [s].[Email], [s].[Gender], [s].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [s].[Name], [s].[Nationality], [s].[Password], [s].[PasswordResetToken], [s].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [s].[PhoneNumber], [s].[Role], [s].[SchoolNumber], [s].[Surname], [s].[TwoFactorEnabled], [s].[TwoFactorSecret]
FROM [Event] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [Club] AS [c] ON [e].[ClubId] = [c].[ClubId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].[ParticipantId], [e0].[EventId], [e0].[RegisteredAt], [e0].[UserId], [u].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[DepartmentId], [u].[DisabilityStatus], [u].[Email], [u].[Gender], [u].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [u].[Name], [u].[Nationality], [u].[Password], [u].[PasswordResetToken], [u].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[Role], [u].[SchoolNumber], [u].[Surname], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[TwoFactorSecret]

SELECT [e].[EventId], [e].[Category], [e].[ClubId], [e].[CreatedAt], [e].[Description], [e].[EndDate], [e].[Image], [e].[ImageUrl], [e].[MaxParticipants], [e].[Name], [e].[ParticipantCount], [e].[StartDate], [e].[Status], [e].[UpdatedAt], [c].[ClubId], [c].[AdvisorId], [c].[CategoryId], [c].[CreatedAt], [c].[Description], [c].[Document], [c].[EventCount], [c].[Image], [c].[MemberCount], [c].[Name], [c].[Status], [s].[ParticipantId], [s].[EventId], [s].[RegisteredAt], [s].[UserId], [s].[UserId0], [s].[CreatedAt], [s].[DepartmentId], [s].[DisabilityStatus], [s].[Email], [s].[Gender], [s].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [s].[Name], [s].[Nationality], [s].[Password], [s].[PasswordResetToken], [s].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [s].[PhoneNumber], [s].[Role], [s].[SchoolNumber], [s].[Surname], [s].[TwoFactorEnabled], [s].[TwoFactorSecret]
FROM [Event] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [Club] AS [c] ON [e].[ClubId] = [c].[ClubId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].[ParticipantId], [e0].[EventId], [e0].[RegisteredAt], [e0].[UserId], [u].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[DepartmentId], [u].[DisabilityStatus], [u].[Email], [u].[Gender], [u].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [u].[Name], [u].[Nationality], [u].[Password], [u].[PasswordResetToken], [u].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[Role], [u].[SchoolNumber], [u].[Surname], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[TwoFactorSecret]
    FROM [EventParticipant] AS [e0]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [e0].[UserId] = [u].[UserId]
) AS [s] ON [e].[EventId] = [s].[EventId]
ORDER BY [e].[EventId], [c].[ClubId], [s].[ParticipantId]

FROM [Event] AS [e]
INNER JOIN [Club] AS [c] ON [e].[ClubId] = [c].[ClubId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [e0].[ParticipantId], [e0].[EventId], [e0].[RegisteredAt], [e0].[UserId], [u].[UserId] AS [UserId0], [u].[CreatedAt], [u].[DepartmentId], [u].[DisabilityStatus], [u].[Email], [u].[Gender], [u].[LastTwoFactorSetup], [u].[Name], [u].[Nationality], [u].[Password], [u].[PasswordResetToken], [u].[PasswordResetTokenExpiry], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[Role], [u].[SchoolNumber], [u].[Surname], [u].[TwoFactorEnabled], [u].[TwoFactorSecret]
    FROM [EventParticipant] AS [e0]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [e0].[UserId] = [u].[UserId]
) AS [s] ON [e].[EventId] = [s].[EventId]
ORDER BY [e].[EventId], [c].[ClubId], [s].[ParticipantId]
